Key:
-Main Series-
 1  : Super Robot Taisen (GB) - 1991
 2  : Dai-2-Ji Super Robot Taisen (NES) - 1991
      Dai-2-Ji Super Robot Taisen (PSX) - 1999
      Famicom Mini: Dai-2-Ji Super Robot Taisen (GBA) - 2004
 2G : Dai-2-Ji Super Robot Taisen G (GB) - 1995
 3  : Dai-3-Ji Super Robot Taisen (SNES) - 1993
      Dai-3-Ji Super Robot Taisen (PSX) - 1999
 EX : Super Robot Taisen EX (SNES) - 1994
      Super Robot Taisen EX (PSX) - 1999
 4  : Dai-4-Ji Super Robot Taisen (SNES) - 1995
      Dai-4-Ji Super Robot Taisen S (PSX) - 1996 (** Exclusives "S" **)
 F  : Super Robot Taisen F (SAT) - 1997
      Super Robot Taisen F (PSX) - 1998
 FF : Super Robot Taisen F Kanketsuhen (SAT) - 1998
      Super Robot Taisen F Kanketsuhen (PSX) - 1999

-Alpha-
 a  : Super Robot Taisen Alpha (PSX) - 2000
      Super Robot Taisen Alpha for Dreamcast (DC) - 2001 (** Exclusives "D" **)
 aG : Super Robot Taisen Alpha Gaiden (PSX) - 2001
 a2 : Dai-2-Ji Super Robot Taisen Alpha (PS2) - 2003
 a3 : Dai-3-Ji Super Robot Taisen Alpha (PS2) - 2005

-Compact Series-
 C1 : Super Robot Taisen Compact (WS) - 1999
      Super Robot Taisen Compact for WonderSwan Color (WSC) - 2001
 C2 : Super Robot Taisen Compact Dai-1-Bu: Chijou Gekidouhen (WS) - 2000
      Super Robot Taisen Compact Dai-2-Bu: Uchuu Gekishinhen (WS) - 2000
      Super Robot Taisen Compact Dai-3-Bu: Ginga Kessenhen (WS) - 2000
 C3 : Super Robot Taisen Compact 3 (WSC) - 2003

-PS2-
 IM : Super Robot Taisen Impact (PS2) - 2002
 MX : Super Robot Taisen MX (PS2) - 2004
      Super Robot Taisen MX Portable (PSP) - 2005

-Z-    
 Z  : Super Robot Taisen Z - 2008
      Super Robot Taisen Z Special Disc - 2009 (** Exclusives "S" **)
 2H : Dai-2-Ji Super Robot Taisen Z Hakaihen - 2011
 
-GBA-
 A  : Super Robot Taisen A (GBA) - 2001 (** Exclusives "A" **)
      Super Robot Taisen A Portable (PSP) - 2008 (** Exclusives "P" **)
 R  : Super Robot Taisen R (GBA) - 2002
 D  : Super Robot Taisen D (GBA) - 2003
 J  : Super Robot Taisen J (GBA) - 2005

-DS-
 W  : Super Robot Taisen W (DS) - 2007
 K  : Super Robot Taisen K (DS) - 2009
 G  : SupaRobo Gakuen (DS) - 2009
 L  : Super Robot Taisen L (DS) - 2010

-Others-
 Sh : Shin Super Robot Taisen (PSX) - 1996
      Shin Super Robot Taisen Special Disc (PSX) - 1997
 64 : Super Robot Taisen 64 (N64) - 1999
      Super Robot Taisen Link Battler (GBC) - 1999
 GC : Super Robot Taisen GC (GC) - 2004 (** Exclusives "G" **)
      Super Robot Taisen XO (360) - 2006 (** Exclusives "O" **)
 N  : Super Robot Taisen Neo (WII) - 2009

-Originals-
 MK : Super Robot Taisen Gaiden: MasouKishin-The Lord of Elemental(SNES) - 1996
      Super Robot Taisen OG Saga: Masou Kishin (DS) - 2010
 OG : Super Robot Taisen Original Generation (GBA) - 2002
 O2 : Super Robot Taisen Original Generation 2 (GBA) - 2004
 OS : Super Robot Taisen Original Generations (PS2) - 2007
    (** 1: OG1 only, 2: OG2 only, 5: OG2.5 only, 3=1+2, 6=1+5, 7=2+5, X=All **)
 GG : Super Robot Taisen Original Generation Gaiden (PS2) - 2007

-1A- : First Appearance
 01-99: Episode/Volume number
 M1-M3: Movie number
 MA: Manga-exclusive
 VA: Variation (aka Gundam MSV series)
 OR: Original (did not appear in anime)

KEY:
X = Full, x = Partial
US: Licensed and readily available in the US on DVD
FS: Available as a fansub, with English subtitles
HK: Available as an HKDVD, with English subtitles
BL: Can be found as a bootleg, dubbed in English  

ADDITIONAL:
1: The Baldios movie exists as an out-of-print VHS dub named "Space Warriors" 
2: The full series and first OVA were released on VHS fully subtitled         
3: A few dubbed episodes were released on VHS as "Macron One"
4: Only the first 15 episodes of 47 were ever released in the US
5: ImaginAsian TV licensed and released an official DVD set of Orguss,       
   but stopped production in May 2008.
6: Licensed in the US, but never released on DVD
7: Never produced, only a 7-minute promo video exists

= IV. nonSRW =
==============

These are series and movies that have yet to appear in a SRW game.. The number
of projects under that name are given in parenthesis after the title. This 
list isn't completely inclusive, and some of the entries aren't really 
"Super" robots, but after the recent inclusion of Tekkaman and Orgun, 
everything is an option.

Missing Music:
--------------
All official music and any named themes should be in and identified. For
games without sound tests (1-2, C1-3, 2G, A, R, D, and OG), there's no 
name for the incidental and original music, unless it gets remade
and named in the next OG. Intentionally not included is the incidental
music in XO and Neo - there's too much to bother with.
 
Compact 2?
-----------
SRW Compact 2 has the exact same character and robot data stored in the
game ROMs for all three games. They've been joined together to save space.
Masaki/Cybuster and Ryuusei/R-1 are in the data, although they're not 
playable.
